date: "2018-07-05"
categories: type-theory

---

This is my attempt to collect in just one-file, a basic overview of HoTT in Agda.
This source code was type-checked by Agda 2.5.4.

Based on:

<div class="references" markdown="1">
- https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/
- https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html
</div>

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT (`--without-K`):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="455" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="459" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="467" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="483" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="488" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="495" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="510" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#518" class="Function">_</a> <a id="520" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="522" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="526" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Universes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword `Set`. It uses `Type` instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="799" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="806" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#806" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="816" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="825" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="891" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="957" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>

Types
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

<a id="1525" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="⊥"></a><a id="1530" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1530" class="Datatype">⊥</a> <a id="1532" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1533" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1533" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1535" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1537" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1544" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1533" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="1547" class="Keyword">where</a>

### Unit

The unit type is defined as record so that we also get the η-rule definitionally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1860" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
<a id="1918" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
<a id="1934" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="⊤"></a><a id="1941" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1941" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1943" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="1951" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="1959" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="⊤.★"></a><a id="1971" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1971" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="unit"></a><a id="1974" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1974" class="Function">unit</a> <a id="1979" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1981" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1971" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="1984" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1988" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> UNIT <a id="2001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1941" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="2003" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

### Σ-types

Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be
constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum
of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in
full generality, at each universe.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2346" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2353" class="Number">60</a> <a id="2356" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2445" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
<a id="2360" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Σ"></a><a id="2367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="2369" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2370" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2375" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2377" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="2389" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="2391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2391" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="2393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2397" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2404" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2406" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2415" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2419" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="2421" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2423" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2425" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="2433" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ._,_"></a><a id="2445" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2445" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
  <a id="2451" class="Keyword">field</a>
    <a id="Σ.fst"></a><a id="2461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="2465" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a>

<a id="2485" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="2490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="2492" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Products (×)

Product type as a particular case of the sigma

### Boolean

Boolean type, two constants true and false

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3099" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Bool"></a><a id="3104" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3104" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="3109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3117" class="Keyword">where</a>

* Booleans can be defined by using a coproduct.

### Natural numbers

Natural numbers are the initial algebra for a constant and a
successor function. The BUILTIN declaration allows us to use
natural numbers in arabic notation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3407" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ"></a><a id="3412" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3422" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ.zero"></a><a id="3430" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3430" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="3435" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="ℕ.succ"></a><a id="3441" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3441" class="InductiveConstructor">succ</a> <a id="3446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3450" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="Nat"></a><a id="3455" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3455" class="Function">Nat</a> <a id="3459" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="3464" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="3468" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> NATURAL <a id="3484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3486" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Common functions

#### Identity function
The identity function with implicit type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="id"></a><a id="3603" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3603" class="Function">id</a> <a id="3606" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3608" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3610" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3611" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3611" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3612" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3614" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3615" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3624" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3611" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3625" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3633" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a>

The identity function on a type `A` is `idf A`.

some errors for my jekyll configuration.

### Identity Type

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5029" class="Comment">-- Equality is defined as an inductive type. Its induction principle</a>

### PathOver

If you have a dependent type `B` over `A`, a path `p : x == y` in `A` and two
points `u : B x` and `v : B y`, there is a **type** `[u == v [ B ↓ p]]` of paths
from `u` to `v` lying over the path `p`.  By definition, if `p` is a constant
path, then `[u == v [ B ↓ p ]]` is just an ordinary path in the fiber.
[More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L115).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="6303" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6303" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="6312" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6314" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6316" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6317" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6317" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="6320" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6320" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6322" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6324" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6325" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6325" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6327" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6334" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6317" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="6336" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6338" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6339" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6339" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6341" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6343" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6325" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6345" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6347" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6352" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6320" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6354" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6477" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="6484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6303" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="6501" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>

## Equational Reasoning

Equational reasoning is a way to write readable chains of equalities.
The idea is that you can write the following:

{% raw %}
```
  t : a == e
  t = a =⟨ p ⟩
      b =⟨ q ⟩
      c =⟨ r ⟩
      d =⟨ s ⟩
      e ∎
```
{% endraw %}

where `p` is a path from `a` to `b`, `q` is a path from `b` to `c`, and so on.
You often have to apply some equality in some context, for instance `p` could be
`ap ctx thm` where `thm` is the interesting theorem used to prove that `a` is
equal to `b`, and `ctx` is the context. [More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L270).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7171" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="7178" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7178" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7198" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7199" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7199" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7201" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7203" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7204" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7204" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7206" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7199" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7215" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7217" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7226" class="Comment">-- Common combinators for equational reasoning. They allow us to</a>
  <a id="7293" class="Comment">-- write proof in an equational style. These versions have been</a>
  <a id="7359" class="Comment">-- adapted from the old version of the HoTT-agda library.</a>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7845" class="Comment">-- Equality.</a>

<a id="7859" class="Comment">-- Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this</a>
<a id="7927" class="Comment">-- is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this</a>
<a id="7995" class="Comment">-- is the symmetric property of equality.</a>
<a id="inv"></a><a id="8037" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8037" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8041" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8043" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8045" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8045" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8046" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8048" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8049" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8049" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8051" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8053" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8058" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8045" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8059" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8062" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8063" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8063" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8065" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8065" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8067" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8069" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8049" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8070" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="8074" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8076" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8063" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8078" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8081" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8065" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="8085" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8065" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8089" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8092" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8063" class="Bound">a</a>

<a id="8117" class="Comment">-- Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions</a>
<a id="8185" class="Comment">-- preserve equalities.</a>

<a id="9338" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9343" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8449" class="Module">·-Properties</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9489" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Transport"></a><a id="9496" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9496" class="Module">Transport</a> <a id="9506" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9507" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9507" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="9509" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9511" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9512" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9512" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9514" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9516" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9521" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9507" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="9523" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9525" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="9533" class="Comment">-- Transport</a>
  <a id="Transport.transport"></a><a id="9548" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9548" class="Function">transport</a> <a id="9558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9560" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9562" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9562" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9564" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9566" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9567" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9567" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9569" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9571" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9512" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9573" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9575" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="9580" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9562" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="9582" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9584" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9585" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9585" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="9587" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9587" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="9589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9591" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9512" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9592" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="9658" class="Comment">-- Some lemmas on the transport operation.</a>
  <a id="Transport.transport-concat-r"></a><a id="9703" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#9703" class="Function">transport-concat-r</a> <a id="9722"     <a id="14379" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14380" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14382" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14384" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14359" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14386" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14361" class="Bound">D</a><a id="14389" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14391" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14394" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14394" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14396" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14398" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14357" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14400" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14359" class="Bound">C</a><a id="14403" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14405" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14407" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14408" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14408" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14410" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14412" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14355" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14414" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14357" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14417" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14419" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="14425" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14427" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14380" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14429" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14431" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14394" class="Bound">g</a><a id="14432" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14434" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14436" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14408" class="Bound">f</a><a id="14437" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14439" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14442" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14443" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14380" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14445" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14447" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14394" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14450" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14408" class="Bound">f</a><a id="14453" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="14458" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14338" class="Function">∘-rassoc</a> <a id="14467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14467" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14469" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14469" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14471" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14471" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14473" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14475" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8037" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="14479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14480" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14173" class="Function">∘-lassoc</a> <a id="14489" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14467" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="14491" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14469" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14493" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14471" class="Bound">f</a><a id="14494" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="14497" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14502" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14133" class="Module">Composition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14669" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="14676" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14676" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="14685" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14686" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14686" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14689" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14689" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14691" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14693" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14694" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14694" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14696" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14698" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14703" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14686" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="14705" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14707" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14708" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14708" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14710" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14712" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14694" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14714" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14716" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14721" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14689" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14723" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14725" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14733" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="14811" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="14851" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14851" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14860" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14862" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14863" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14863" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14865" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14865" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14867" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14869" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14871" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14871" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14873" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14875" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14694" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14876" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14878" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14880" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14708" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14882" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14871" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14883" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14886" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14888" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14893" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14894" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14686" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14897" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14899" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14689" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14901" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14905" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14851" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14914" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14914" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14916" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14916" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14918" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14920" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14921" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14921" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14923" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14925" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14694" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14926" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14928" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14930" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14914" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14932" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14921" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14934" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14937" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14916" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14939" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14921" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="Homotopy._∼_"></a><a id="14944" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14944" class="Function Operator">_∼_</a> <a id="14948" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14950" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14951" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14951" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14953" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14953" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14955" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14957" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14959" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14959" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14961" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14963" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14694" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14964" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14966" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14968" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14708" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14970" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14959" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14971" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14974" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14976" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14981" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14982" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14686" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14985" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14987" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14689" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14989" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14993" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14993" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14995" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14944" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="14997" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14997" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14999" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14851" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15010" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14993" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15012" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14997" class="Bound">g</a>

<a id="15915" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15920" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15482" class="Module">HomotopyComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

  <a id="17207" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7615" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Fibers

Contractible types with a center of contraction.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17295" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Fibers"></a><a id="17302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17302" class="Module">Fibers</a> <a id="17309" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17310" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17310" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="17313" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17313" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="17315" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17317" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17318" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17318" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="17320" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17322" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="17327" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17310" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="17329" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17331" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17332" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17332" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="17334" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17336" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="17341" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17313" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="17343" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="17346" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Contractible types

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17824" class="Comment">-- Contractible.  Contractible types with a center of contraction.</a>
<a id="17891" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Contractible"></a><a id="17898" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17898" class="Module">Contractible</a> <a id="17911" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="17920" class="Comment">-- Contractible types. A contractible type is a type such that every</a>
  <a id="17991" class="Comment">-- element is equal to a center of contraction.</a>

## Equivalence in HoTT

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="18201" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Equivalence"></a><a id="18208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18208" class="Module">Equivalence</a> <a id="18220" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="18229" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DefinitionOfEquivalence"></a><a id="18236" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18236" class="Module">DefinitionOfEquivalence</a> <a id="18260" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18261" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18261" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18264" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18264" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18266" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18268" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18269" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18269" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18271" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18273" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18278" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18261" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="18280" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18282" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18283" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18283" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="18285" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18292" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18264" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18294" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18296" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="18306" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="18374" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="18439" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="18456" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18456" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18469" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18470" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18470" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18472" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18474" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18269" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18476" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18478" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18283" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18479" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18481" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18483" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18489" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18261" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18492" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18494" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18264" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18496" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="18502" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18456" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18513" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18513" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18515" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18517" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18518" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="18520" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18522" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18283" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18523" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18525" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18527" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18041" class="Function">isContr</a> <a id="18535" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18536" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#17404" class="Function">fib</a> <a id="18540" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18513" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18542" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18518" class="Bound">b</a><a id="18543" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="18550" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="18621" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isEquiv"></a><a id="18664" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18664" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="18672" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18674" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18675" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18675" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18677" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18679" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18269" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18681" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18683" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18283" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18684" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18686" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18688" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18693" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18694" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18261" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18697" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18699" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18264" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18701" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="18707" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18664" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="18715" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18717" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18456" class="Function">isContrMap</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21973" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="21980" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21980" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="21997" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21998" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21998" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="22001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22001" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22003" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22005" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22006" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22006" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22008" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22010" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22015" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#21998" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="22017" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22019" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22020" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22020" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="22022" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22024" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22029" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22001" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22031" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22033" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22042" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>
  <a id="22109" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>
  <a id="CartesianProduct.prodComponentwise"></a><a id="22155" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22155" class="Function">prodComponentwise</a> <a id="22173" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22175" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22176" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22176" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22178" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22178" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="22180" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22182" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22006" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22184" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="22186" href="{% endraw %}{% link ## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23158" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="23165" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23165" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="23183" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23184" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23184" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23185" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23187" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="23196" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="23267" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="23305" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23305" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23311" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23313" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23314" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23314" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23316" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23318" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23323" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23184" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23324" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23326" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23328" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23333" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23184" class="Bound">ℓ</a>

<a id="23870" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="23875" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23165" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24105" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="24112" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24112" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="24125" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24134" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="24203" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="24218" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24218" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24225" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24227" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24229" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24230" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="24233" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24234" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24234" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24238" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24243" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24229" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24244" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24246" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24248" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24253" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24229" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="24257" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24218" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24264" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24264" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24266" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24268" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24270" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24270" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24272" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24272" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="24274" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24276" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24264" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24277" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24279" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24281" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24270" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24283" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5141" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24286" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24272" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24287" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24292" class="Comment">-- The type of mere propositions</a>
  <a id="Propositions.hProp"></a><a id="24327" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24327" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24335" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24337" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24337" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24338" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24340" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24342" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24347" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24348" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="24353" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24337" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24354" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24327" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24364" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24365" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24366" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24368" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24370" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24372" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24365" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24379" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24381" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24218" class="Function">isProp</a>


  <a id="24392" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="24458" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.piProp"></a><a id="24476" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24476" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24483" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24485" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24487" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24487" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24490" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24492" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24494" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24496" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24497" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24497" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24499" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24501" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24506" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24487" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24508" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24510" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24512" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24513" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24513" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24515" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24517" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24497" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24519" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24521" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24526" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24490" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24528" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="24539" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24541" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24543" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24543" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24545" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24547" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24497" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24548" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24550" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24552" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24218" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24559" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24560" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24513" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24562" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24543" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24563" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24566" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24568" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24218" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24575" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24577" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24577" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24579" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24581" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24497" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24582" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24584" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24586" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24513" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24588" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24577" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24589" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24593" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24476" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24600" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24600" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24606" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24606" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24608" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24608" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24610" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24612" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20303" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="24619" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24621" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24621" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24623" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24625" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24600" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24631" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24621" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24633" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24634" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24606" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24636" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24621" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24637" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24639" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24640" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24608" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24642" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24621" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24643" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24648" class="Comment">-- The product of propositions is itself a proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="24706" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24706" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="24718" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24720" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24722" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24722" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24725" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24725" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24727" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24729" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24731" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24732" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24732" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24734" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24736" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24741" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24722" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24743" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24745" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24747" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24748" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24748" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24752" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24757" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24725" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24759" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="24775" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24777" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24218" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24784" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24732" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24786" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24788" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24218" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24795" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24748" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24797" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24799" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24218" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24806" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24807" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24732" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24809" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24811" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24748" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24812" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="24876" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24881" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24112" class="Module">Propositions</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25089" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="25096" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25096" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="25101" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25110" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="25181" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>

     <a id="25545" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25528" class="Bound">p</a>

<a id="25796" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25801" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25096" class="Module">Sets</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

<a id="28064" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28069" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27282" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28313" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="28320" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28320" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="28333" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28334" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28334" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28337" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28337" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28339" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28341" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28342" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28342" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28344" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28346" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28351" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28334" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="28353" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28355" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28356" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28356" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28358" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28337" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28367" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28369" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="28378" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>
  <a id="28409" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Halfadjoints.ishae"></a><a id="28416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28416" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="28422" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28423" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28423" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28425" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28427" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28342" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28429" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28431" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28356" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28432" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28434" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28436" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28441" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28442" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28334" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28445" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="28447" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28337" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28449" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28451" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31170" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="31177" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31177" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="31191" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31192" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31192" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="31195" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31195" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31197" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31199" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31200" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31200" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31202" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31204" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31209" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31192" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="31211" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31213" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31214" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="31216" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31218" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31223" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31195" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31225" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31227" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="33923" class="Comment">-- Half-adjoint equivalences are quasiinverses.</a>

   <a id="35331" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7670" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
     <a id="35342" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35346" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35347" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34788" class="Function">compEqv</a> <a id="35355" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35314" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="35357" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35000" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35314" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35366" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="35369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7516" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5188" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="35378" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="35380" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7516" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35391" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35392" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35000" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35314" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35400" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="35404" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35408" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35314" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="35414" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7516" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35418" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20303" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="35425" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35426" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19572" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="35442" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35314" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35443" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35445" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7516" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3603" class="Function">id</a>
   <a id="35458" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7615" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="35459" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="35462" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="35467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34208" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="35680" class="Comment">-- module Univalence where</a>
<a id="35707" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="35710" class="Comment">--   -- Voevodsky&#39;s Univalence Axiom.</a>
<a id="35748" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceAxiom {ℓ} {A B : Type ℓ} where</a>
<a id="35801" class="Comment">--     idtoeqv : A == B → A ≃ B</a>
<a id="35833" class="Comment">--     idtoeqv p = qinv-≃</a>
<a id="35859" class="Comment">--       (transport (λ x → x) p)</a>
<a id="35892" class="Comment">--       (transport (λ x → x) (inv p) , (transport-inv-l p , transport-inv-r p))</a>
<a id="35973" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="35976" class="Comment">--     -- The Univalence axiom induces an equivalence between equalities</a>
<a id="36049" class="Comment">--     -- and equivalences.</a>
<a id="36077" class="Comment">--     postulate axiomUnivalence : isEquiv idtoeqv</a>
<a id="36128" class="Comment">--     eqvUnivalence : (A == B) ≃ (A ≃ B)</a>
<a id="36170" class="Comment">--     eqvUnivalence = idtoeqv , axiomUnivalence</a>
<a id="36219" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36222" class="Comment">--     -- Introduction rule for equalities.</a>
<a id="36266" class="Comment">--     ua : A ≃ B → A == B</a>
<a id="36293" class="Comment">--     ua = remap eqvUnivalence</a>
<a id="36325" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36328" class="Comment">--     -- Computation rules</a>
<a id="36356" class="Comment">--     ua-β : (eqv : A ≃ B) → idtoeqv (ua eqv) == eqv</a>
<a id="36410" class="Comment">--     ua-β eqv = lrmap-inverse eqvUnivalence</a>
<a id="36456" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36459" class="Comment">--     ua-η : (p : A == B) → ua (idtoeqv p) == p</a>
<a id="36508" class="Comment">--     ua-η p = rlmap-inverse eqvUnivalence</a>
<a id="36552" class="Comment">--   open UnivalenceAxiom public</a>
<a id="36585" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36588" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36591" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="36630" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="36691" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="36740" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="36759" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="36774" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="36839" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="36892" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="36910" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="36921" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36924" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="36996" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="37021" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37117" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="37138" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="37153" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37260" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="37365" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37444" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="37520" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37603" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37626" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="37637" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="37652" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="37738" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="37767" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="37786" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ fst (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="37874" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37984" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="38072" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="38115" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="38131" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38134" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="38168" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="38248" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="38268" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38283" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="38353" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38418" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="38467" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="38485" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="38496" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38499" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
<a id="38574" class="Comment">--     ua-inv α =</a>
<a id="38592" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38607" class="Comment">--         ua (invEqv α)                       ==⟨ ap (_· ua (invEqv α)) (inv (·-linv (ua α))) ⟩</a>
<a id="38704" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · ua α · ua (invEqv α)   ==⟨ ·-assoc (inv (ua α)) _ _ ⟩</a>
<a id="38782" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · (ua α · ua (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap (inv (ua α) ·_) (ua-inv-r α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38867" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α) · refl _                 ==⟨ inv (·-runit (inv ((ua α)))) ⟩</a>
<a id="38949" class="Comment">--         inv (ua α)</a>
<a id="38971" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="38982" class="Comment">--   open UnivalenceLemmas public</a>
<a id="39016" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="39019" class="Comment">-- open Univalence</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
